def get_space():
    return {
        'dropout_rate': hp.uniform('dropout_rate', 0, 0.5),
        'dropout_rate_1': hp.uniform('dropout_rate_1', 0, 0.5),
        'lr': hp.uniform('lr', 0.0001, 0.01),
        'layer': hp.choice('layer', config.neurons),
        'layer_1': hp.choice('layer_1', config.neurons_1),
        'layer_2': hp.choice('layer_2', config.neurons_2),
        'batch_size': hp.choice('batch_size', [ 128,256,512]),
    }

>>> Functions
   1: def siamese_base_model(input_shape, first_drop, second_drop, first_layer, second_layer, third_layer, add_fourth_layer):
   2:     """
   3:     Function creating the common base for the siamese network
   4:     :param input_shape: the shape of the input for the first layer
   5:     :param first_drop: a float between 0 and 1 indicating first dropout layer's drop rate
   6:     :param second_drop: a float between 0 and 1 indicating second dropout layer's drop rate
   7:     :param first_layer: a positive integer indicating the number of neurons of the first layer
   8:     :param second_layer: a positive integer indicating the number of neurons of the second layer
   9:     :param third_layer: a positive integer indicating the number of neurons of the third layer
  10:     :param add_fourth_layer: a boolean indicating whether to add (True) or not (False) the fourth layer consisting of
  11:                             a Dense layer with 512 neurons and sigmoid activation function
  12:     :return: a Model with three dense layers interspersed with two dropout layers
  13:     """
  14:     input_layer = Input(input_shape)
  15:     hidden = Dense(first_layer, activation='relu')(input_layer)
  16:     hidden = Dropout(first_drop)(hidden)
  17:     hidden = Dense(second_layer, activation='relu')(hidden)
  18:     hidden = Dropout(second_drop)(hidden)
  19:     hidden = Dense(third_layer, activation='relu')(hidden)
  20:     if add_fourth_layer is True:
  21:         hidden = Dense(512, activation='sigmoid')(hidden)
  22:     return Model(input_layer, hidden)
  23: 
  24: def siamese_model(train_set, train_labels, test_set, test_labels, score_function):
  25:     """
  26:     Function for creating and testing a siamese model, given the training and the test set as input.
  27:     This function is used inside hyperparam_search, in order to find the model with the best hyper-parameters
  28:     :param train_set: the training set for the model. It is assumed to be an array of preprocessed pixel pairs
  29:     :param train_labels: a 1-dim array containing the training labels. it is assumed it's the same length of train_set
  30:     :param test_set: the test set for the model. The assumption are the same of train_set
  31:     :param test_labels: a 1-dim array containing the test labels for metrics computation. it is assumed it's the same
  32:                         length of test_set
  33:     :param score_function: the function to be used for calculating distances. it can be SAM or euclidean_distance
  34:     :return: a compiled siamese model with adam optimization
  35:     """
  36:     # building the net
  37:     input_shape = train_set[0, 0].shape
  38:     dropout_rate = {{uniform(0, 0.5)}}
  39:     dropout_rate_1 = {{uniform(0, 0.5)}}
  40:     lr = {{uniform(0.0001, 0.01)}}
  41:     layer = {{choice(config.neurons)}}
  42:     layer_1 = {{choice(config.neurons_1)}}
  43:     layer_2 = {{choice(config.neurons_2)}}
  44: 
  45:     param = {'dropout_rate': dropout_rate,
  46:              'dropout_rate_1': dropout_rate_1,
  47:              'lr': lr,
  48:              'layer': layer,
  49:              'layer_1': layer_1,
  50:              'layer_2': layer_2,
  51:              'score_function': score_function,
  52:              'margin': config.AVAILABLE_MARGIN[score_function.__name__],
  53:              'fourth_layer': config.fourth_layer}
  54: 
  55:     siamese = build_net(input_shape, param)
  56: 
  57:     # setting an EarlyStopping callback
  58:     callbacks_list = [
  59:         callbacks.EarlyStopping(monitor='val_loss', min_delta=0.0001, patience=10,
  60:                                 restore_best_weights=True),
  61:     ]
  62: 
  63:     # generating the validation set
  64:     x_train, x_val, y_train, y_val = train_test_split(train_set, train_labels, stratify=train_labels,
  65:                                                       test_size=config.VAL_SPLIT)
  66: 
  67:     tic = time.time()
  68:     # fitting the model
  69:     try:
  70:         h = siamese.fit([x_train[:, 0], x_train[:, 1]], y_train,
  71:                         batch_size={{choice([ 128,256,512])}}, #32, 64, 128, 256, 512])}},
  72:                         epochs=150,
  73:                         verbose=2,
  74:                         callbacks=callbacks_list,
  75:                         validation_data=([x_val[:, 0], x_val[:, 1]], y_val))
  76:     except:
  77:         print("Error in training")
  78:         config.test_cm.append(np.zeros(shape=(2, 2)))
  79:         config.val_cm.append(np.zeros(shape=(2, 2)))
  80:         return {'status': STATUS_FAIL}
  81: 
  82:     toc = time.time()
  83:     # printing the best score
  84:     best_epoch_idx = np.nanargmin(h.history['val_loss'])
  85:     # the score returned is the best epoch one
  86:     loss = h.history['loss'][best_epoch_idx]
  87:     score = h.history['val_loss'][best_epoch_idx]
  88:     val_acc = h.history['val_accuracy'][best_epoch_idx]
  89: 
  90:     print('Score: ' + str(score))
  91:     print('Loss: ' + str(loss))
  92:     print('Validation Accuracy: ' + str(val_acc))
  93:     print('Epochs: ' + str(len(h.history['loss'])))
  94: 
  95:     # making prediction on the test set
  96:     distances = siamese.predict([test_set[:, 0], test_set[:, 1]])
  97: 
  98:     test_thresh = threshold_otsu(distances)
  99:     # converting distances into labels
 100:     prediction = np.where(distances.ravel() > test_thresh, config.CHANGED_LABEL, config.UNCHANGED_LABEL)
 101:     cm = skm.confusion_matrix(test_labels, prediction, labels=[config.CHANGED_LABEL, config.UNCHANGED_LABEL])
 102:     config.test_cm.append(cm)
 103: 
 104:     # making preditcion on the validation set
 105:     val_distances = siamese.predict([x_val[:, 0], x_val[:, 1]])
 106: 
 107:     val_thresh = threshold_otsu(val_distances)
 108:     # converting distances into labels
 109:     val_prediction = np.where(val_distances.ravel() > val_thresh, config.CHANGED_LABEL, config.UNCHANGED_LABEL)
 110:     vcm = skm.confusion_matrix(y_val, val_prediction, labels=[config.CHANGED_LABEL, config.UNCHANGED_LABEL])
 111:     config.val_cm.append(vcm)
 112: 
 113:     print('test threshold: ' + str(test_thresh))
 114:     print('val threshold: ' + str(val_thresh))
 115:     print('Best Score: ', str(config.best_score))
 116:     if score < config.best_score:
 117:         config.best_score = score
 118:         config.best_model = siamese
 119:         config.best_time = toc - tic
 120: 
 121:     return {'loss': score, 'status': STATUS_OK, 'n_epochs': len(h.history['loss']),
 122:             'model': config.best_model, 'time': toc - tic, 'cont_loss': loss, 'val_cont_loss': score,
 123:             'test_thresh': test_thresh, 'val_thresh': val_thresh}
 124: 
 125: def build_net(input_shape, parameters):
 126:     """
 127:     Function building the architecture for the net. Because of the Lambda layer, the net cant' be serialized as
 128:     a saved_model, so it must be rebuilt each time.
 129: 
 130:     :param input_shape: the shape for the input layer
 131:     :param parameters: dict, contains the parameter for building the network:
 132:         'dropout_rate': the rate for the first dropout layer
 133:         'dropout_rate_1': the rate for the second dropout layer. The name is given
 134:                             by the hyperas optimization process
 135:         'lr': the learning rate
 136:         'layer': the number of neurons for the first dense layer
 137:         'layer_1': the number of neurons for the second dense layer
 138:         'layer_2': the number of neurons for the third dense layer
 139:         'score_function': the name of the score function selected for the net
 140:         'margin': a float indicating the margin to be used for the contrastive loss function
 141:         'fourth_layer': a boolean indicating whether to add or not the fourth layer to the base model, consisting
 142:                        of a Dense layer with 512 neurons and sigmoid activation function
 143:     :return: a compiled keras model with the given parameters
 144:     """
 145:     base = siamese_base_model(input_shape, parameters['dropout_rate'], parameters['dropout_rate_1'],
 146:                               parameters['layer'], parameters['layer_1'], parameters['layer_2'],
 147:                               parameters['fourth_layer'])
 148: 
 149:     input_a = Input(input_shape)
 150:     input_b = Input(input_shape)
 151: 
 152:     joined_ia = base(input_a)
 153:     joined_ib = base(input_b)
 154: 
 155:     distance_layer = Lambda(parameters['score_function'])([joined_ia, joined_ib])
 156:     siamese = Model([input_a, input_b], distance_layer)
 157: 
 158:     adam = Adam(lr=parameters['lr'])
 159:     siamese.compile(loss=contrastive_loss, optimizer=adam, metrics=[accuracy])
 160:     config.MARGIN = parameters['margin']
 161:     siamese.summary()
 162:     return siamese
 163: 
 164: def contrastive_loss(y_true, y_pred):
 165:     """
 166:     Function implementing the contrastive loss for the training phase
 167:     :param y_true: the actual value for the pixel's class (1 not changed = same class, 0 changed = different class)
 168:     :param y_pred: the predicted value for the pixel's class
 169:     :return: the value of the contrastive loss. The margin, positive value which helps to make largely
 170:     dissimilar pairs to count toward the loss computation, is stored in config.py
 171:     """
 172:     y_true = tf.cast(y_true, y_pred.dtype)
 173:     square_pred = kb.square(y_pred)
 174:     square_margin = kb.square(kb.maximum(config.MARGIN - y_pred, 0))
 175:     return kb.mean(y_true * square_pred + (1 - y_true) * square_margin)
 176: 
 177: def SAM(tens):
 178:     """
 179:     Function defining the Spectral Angle Mapper score to be applied
 180:     on the result of the Siamese Branches
 181:     :param tens: the two tensors (spectral signature of each pixel) to be compared
 182:     :return: the SAM score between the tensors as arccos(t1xt2/norm2(t1)*norm2(t2))
 183:     """
 184:     (x, y) = tens
 185:     xnorm = kb.l2_normalize(x, axis=1)
 186:     ynorm = kb.l2_normalize(y, axis=1)
 187:     dot = kb.sum(xnorm * ynorm, axis=1, keepdims=True)
 188:     # dot must be bounded since some values could a little bit more than 1 or less than -1
 189:     dot = kb.maximum(dot, -1)
 190:     dot = kb.minimum(dot, 1)
 191:     return tf.math.acos(dot)
 192: 
 193: def accuracy(y_true, y_pred):
 194:     """
 195:     Function computing the training accuracy
 196:     :param y_true: the actual value for the pixel's class (1 not changed = same class, 0 changed = different class)
 197:     :param y_pred: the predicted value for the pixel's class
 198:     :return: the accuracy considering y_pred = 1 <=> y_pred<0.5
 199:     """
 200:     return kb.mean(kb.equal(y_true, kb.cast(y_pred < config.PRED_THRESHOLD, y_true.dtype)))
